GT Equivalence Verification (CRK20)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_p*sin(c3*A)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT:** `-0.3122*A*exp(-0.07984*t) + 0.4717*sin(0.8722*A)`

The GT has two terms:
1. A term proportional to `A*exp(-αt)` (exponential decay in t, linear in A)
2. A term proportional to `sin(βA)` (sinusoidal in A, no t-dependence)

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

**Key observations about GT structure:**
- It contains `A*exp(ct)` — linear in A times exponential in t
- It contains `sin(cA)` — sine of a linear function of A
- No polynomial terms in A (no A², A³, etc.)
- No constant offset term
- No terms involving t alone

Let me check each candidate:

### Candidate 1:
`A²c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3/(A*c4+1) + A*c5/(A+c6) + A*c7*sin(c8*t+c9)`

Has `A*exp(ct)` ✓. But the sin term is `sin(c8*t+c9)` — sinusoidal in t, not in A. The GT needs `sin(cA)`. The rational terms `A*c3/(A*c4+1)` and `A*c5/(A+c6)` can approximate but never exactly equal `sin(cA)`. Setting c0=0, c3=0, c5=0, c7=0 leaves only `A*c1*exp(c2*t)`, missing the sin term.

Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 2:
`A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2/(A*c3+1) + A*c4/(A+c5) + A*c6*log(c7*|A|+1) + c8*|A|/(c9*|A|+1)²`

Has `A*exp(ct)` ✓. But no `sin(cA)` term. Rational functions and log cannot produce sin.

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 3:
`A*c0 + c1*t*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t)*log(A*c6+1)*sin(c7*t+c8)`

Has a coupled term `exp(c5*t)*log(A*c6+1)*sin(c7*t+c8)`. This mixes t and A in a way GT doesn't. The GT's sin term has no t-dependence. Setting c4=0 kills the sin entirely. No pure `sin(cA)` term available.

Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 4:
`A*c0 + c1*t^c2 + c3*exp(c4*t)*cos(c5*t) + c6*(c7*|A|+1)^(c8*cos(c9*t))`

Complex structure. The last term has t-dependent exponent on an A-dependent base. Cannot produce `sin(cA)` or `A*exp(ct)`.

Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 5:
`A*c0/(A+c1) + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*(A*c6)^c7)`

No `A*exp(ct)` term (the exp terms are either pure t or pure A). No `sin(cA)`. Cannot match.

Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 6:
`A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2/(A*c3+1) + A*c4/(A+c5) + c6*exp(c7*t)*log(A*c8+1)`

Has `A*exp(ct)` ✓. But no `sin(cA)`. The remaining terms are rational in A and log*exp. Cannot produce sin.

Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 7:
`A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2/(A*c3+1) + A*c4/(A+c5) + c6*exp(c7*t)*log(c8*|A|+1)`

Same issue as Candidate 6. No sin term.

Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 8:
`A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*t*exp(c6*t) + c7/(A^5*|(A+c8)^5|)`

No sin term.

Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 9:
`A²c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c5*(c6+t)^c7 + c8*log(A*c9+1)`

Has `A*exp(ct)` ✓. But no `sin(cA)`. log cannot equal sin.

Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 10:
`A*c0 + A*c1 + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5 + c6*exp(c7*t) + c8*exp(c9*t)`

No sin term. `A^c2*exp(c4*t)` with c2=1 gives `A*exp(ct)` ✓, but still no sin.

Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 11:
`A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2*t^c3 + A*c4/(A*c5+1) + c6*exp(c7*t)*log(A*c8+1)`

No sin term.

Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 12:
`A*c0 + c1*t*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*exp(c7*t)*sin(c8*t+c9)`

Sin is in t, not A. No `A*exp(ct)` term. Cannot match.

Candidate 12 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 13:
`A²c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/√(c3+t) + A*c4 + A*c5/(A+c6) + c7*exp(c8*t)`

No sin term. `A/√(c3+t)` is not `A*exp(ct)`.

Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 14:
`A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2 + c3*log(c4*exp(A^c5*c6)+1) + c7*Max(0,A) + c8*exp(c9*t)/A^5`

Has `A*exp(ct)` ✓. The log(c4*exp(A^c5*c6)+1) term — if c5=1, this is log(c4*exp(c6*A)+1), which is a softplus-like function, not sin. Cannot produce sin.

Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 15:
`A²c0 + A*c1 + c2*sin(c3*log(c4*|A|+1)+c5)`

No t-dependence at all! The GT has `A*exp(-0.08t)` which depends on t. Setting c0=0, c1=0 leaves only the sin term, but we lose the t-dependent part. Cannot match.

Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 42:
`A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2/(A*c3+1) + A*c4/(A+c5) + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8+1)+c9)`

Has `A*exp(ct)` ✓. Has `sin(c7*log(A*c8+1)+c9)`. 

The question is: can `sin(c7*log(c8*A+1))` equal `sin(βA)` for all A≥0?

This requires `c7*log(c8*A+1) + c9 = βA + 2πn` for all A, which means `log(c8*A+1) = (β/c7)*A + const`. But log(c8*A+1) is logarithmic while the RHS is linear. These are not equal for all A.

Also need to handle the rational terms. Setting c2=0, c4=0 leaves `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*A+1)+c9)`. The sin argument is wrong.

Candidate 42 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 43:
`A²c0 + A²c1 + A*c2 + A*c3 + A*c4 + A*c5/(A+c6) + c7*t*exp(c8*t) + c9`

No sin, no `A*exp(ct)`.

## Summary

None of the candidates contain both:
1. An `A*exp(ct)` term (or equivalent t-dependent term matching exponential decay times A)
2. A `sin(cA)` term (sine of a linear function of A)

The closest candidates have `sin(log(A))` instead of `sin(A)`, or have `sin(t)` instead of `sin(A)`, or are missing the sin entirely.
